 giraftaar kiye gaye nau logon main thane mahapalika ke nilambit up mahapalika ayukta deepak chavaan, sahaayak mahapalika ayukta (eemasi) babasaheb andhaale, mahapalika nigam ke lipic kiran madke, rashtravaadi congress party (rakanpa) ke karporator hira patil, pulicekarmi saiyad, chavaan ke 'sangraahak' estate agent jabbaar patel ke alaava ek purv eemasi therbhole bhi shaamil hai jinhen ravivaar dopaher ko giraftaar kiya gaya
 Two builders Jamil Qureshi and Salim Sheikh have been arrested by the police from Uttar Pradesh and Thane respectively on Saturday
 rakanpa ke pradesh adhyaksh madhukarrav pichaad ne ravivaar ko party ke karporator hira patil ko nilambit kiye jane kii ghoshnaa kii
 All the arrested people have been charged with culpable homicide

 Indian cricket team captain Mahendra Singh Dhoni said on Tuesday that his teammates are fully prepared for the mahamukabale to be held with Pakistan on Wednesday
 captain ne kaha ki is match ko lekar donon deshon main jabardast charchaa or utsaah he, lekin unke saathi in tamaam charchaaon se 'bekhbar' abhyaas par dhyaan lagaae hue hai
 Dhoni told reporters on the eve of the ICC World Cup-2011 semi-final match to be held at the Punjab Cricket Association (PCA) ground with Pakistan, ‚Äúit is definitely a big match for us
 ek to yah semifinal he or duusare, hamaara saamana pakistan se hona he
 There is a lot of discussion about this match, but we are not impressed by it
 hamaara dhyaan apane kaam par he
 We are building on match by match strategy
 media ke madhyam se jo baaten saamne aa rahi hai, usase bekhbar mere sabhi saathi apni bhoomika ko shreshthata se anjaam tak pahunchane main jute hue hai
 "dhoni said that the 'hype' about this match has been prepared by the media and sponsors
 isse team ko koi fark nahin padataa
 Dhoni said, "look, i want to make it clear that we are not involved in the hype media and sponsors have created
 ab tak kul saat sawaal isi hip ko lekar puche ja chuke hai
 We promise to play good cricket
 ham maidan main yahi kar sakate hai
 It is not our job to be involved in the discussion, because we will get nothing from it
 " captain ne kaha ki team ke sabhi sadsy feet hai or mangalvaar dopaher ke abhyaas ke baad ve sidhe match ke liye hi maidan main utrenge
 Dhoni said, "the good news for us is that all our players are fit
" is match ke liye ham puri tarah apni kshamtaaon par dhyaan de rahe hai or unhen maanjane ke liye mehnat kar rahe hai
 We are dependent on our fitness and technique and we hope that this will definitely give us positive results
 " pakistani team ke bare main puche jane par bhartiya captain ne kaha ki beete dinon main is team ne shandaar pradarshan kiya he or khud ko khitaab ke daavedaaron main shaamil kiya he
 According to the captain, the Pakistan team has some good all-rounders, which provide them a great balance
 captain bole, "pakistan team ke paas kuch achche harfanmaulaa khilaadi hai
 This gives him the freedom to field with five bowlers
